#   Â© Copyright IBM Corp. 2020, 2023
#
#
#   The following data demonstrates an example of subset of CiscoACI fabric topology environment.
#
#   In general, resources observed by the CiscoACI observer on fabric topology consists of following objects:
#
#   (1) fabricInst              - A container group object for fabric policies
#   (2) fabricNode              - The root node for the APIC
#   (3) polUni                  - Represents policy definition or resolution universe
#   (4) firmwareRunning         - Information about leaf or spine switch firmware running on a node
#   (5) firmwareCtrlrRunning    - Information about each controller firmware that is running
#   (6) eqptLCSlot              - The slot for the module card
#   (7) eqptLC                  - A line card (IO card) contains IO ports
#   (8) eqptPsuSlot             - The power supply slot
#   (9) eqptPsu                 - The power supply unit
#  (10) eqptFtSlot              - A fan tray slot
#  (11) eqptFan                 - The fan in a fan tray
#  (12) mgmtMgmtIf              - The management interface
#  (13) cnwPhysIf               - The physical interface assigned to the node cluster
#  (14) l1PhysIf                - The object that represents the Layer 1 physical Ethernet interface information object
#  (15) mgmtRsOoBStNode         - An object which contains management ip address of fabric spine switches and fabric leaf switches
#
#   For complete reference of Cisco ACI objects, please refer to https://developer.cisco.com/docs/apic-mim-ref/
#
#   a) Container group fabricInst is managed by policy polUni
#   b) fabricInst have one or more fabricNode which is made up of APIC, leaf and spine
#   c) fabricNode APIC contains the following resource:
#         - firmwareCtrlrRunning
#         - cnwPhysIf
#         - eqptPsuSlot
#         - eqptPsu
#         - eqptFtSlot
#         - eqptFan
#   c) Both fabricNode leaf and spine contains the following resource:
#         - firmwareRunning
#         - mgmtMgmtIf
#         - mgmtRsOoBStNode
#         - eqptPsuSlot
#         - eqptPsu
#         - eqptFtSlot
#         - eqptFan
#         - eqptLCSlot
#         - eqptLC
#         - l1PhysIf
#
#   To illustrate the above, let's choose a specific example:
#
#   a) Container group 'uni'(fabricInst) is managed by policy 'uni/fabric'(polUni)
#   b) 'uni'(fabricInst) have fabricNode APIC called 'apic1', fabricNode leaf '101leaf' and fabricNode spine '201spine'
#   c) 'apic1' contains the following resource:
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-1/sys/ctrlrfwstatuscont/ctrlrrunning' (firmwareCtrlrRunning)
#         - 'eth1/1'                                                   (cnwPhysIf)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-1/sys/ch/psuslot-5'                   (eqptPsuSlot)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-1/sys/ch/psuslot-5/psu'               (eqptPsu)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-1/sys/ch/ftslot-4'                    (eqptFtSlot)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-1/sys/ch/ftslot-4/ft/fan-1'           (eqptFan)
#
#   c) 101leaf' fabricNode leaf contains the following resource:
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-101/sys/fwstatuscont/running'         (firmwareRunning)
#         - 'mgmt0'                                                    (mgmtMgmtIf)
#         - '172.21.23.134'                                            (mgmtRsOoBStNode)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-101/sys/ch/psuslot-1'                 (eqptPsuSlot)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-101/sys/ch/psuslot-1/psu'             (eqptPsu)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-101/sys/ch/ftslot-1'                  (eqptFtSlot)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-101/sys/ch/ftslot-1/ft/fan-1'         (eqptFan)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-101/sys/ch/lcslot-1'                  (eqptLCSlot)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-101/sys/ch/lcslot-1/lc'               (eqptLC)
#         - 'eth1/1'                                                   (l1PhysIf)
#
#   c) '201spine' fabricNode spine contains the following resource:
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-201/sys/fwstatuscont/running'         (firmwareRunning)
#         - 'mgmt0'                                                    (mgmtMgmtIf)
#         - '172.21.23.136'                                            (mgmtRsOoBStNode)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-201/sys/ch/psuslot-1'                 (eqptPsuSlot)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-201/sys/ch/psuslot-1/psu'             (eqptPsu)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-201/sys/ch/ftslot-1'                  (eqptFtSlot)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-201/sys/ch/ftslot-1/ft/fan-1'         (eqptFan)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-201/sys/ch/lcslot-1'                  (eqptLCSlot)
#         - 'topology/pod-1/node-201/sys/ch/lcslot-1/lc'               (eqptLC)
#         - 'eth1/2'                                                   (l1PhysIf)
#
#
